## Instruction

In the table of the Notion page `mcp_experiments_recordings`, based on the historical experiments of W&B project `mbzuai-llm/Guru`, list the highest val-core acc mean@1/mean@k scores for each benchmark according to the table headers, and calculate and fill in the Best Step for that run (format: step(average acc)).

Instructions:

- If multiple runs have the same name, treat them as one run for combined statistics.
- The average score should only be calculated using the arithmetic mean of metrics available at that step; missing metrics are not included.
- Only operate on the target page under the specified parent page; do not change column names or order.

```python
}

print("Runs in the project:")
for i, run in enumerate(runs_data):
    print(f"{i+1}. {run['name']} - {run['displayName']} ({run['state']})")

print(f"\nTotal runs: {len(runs_data)}")
print(f"Notion columns to map: {len(notion_columns)}") code
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
import json
import re
from collections import defaultdict

# First, let me create a function to extract val-core metrics from summary data
def extract_val_core_metrics(summary_json_str):
    """Extract val-core metrics from a summary JSON string"""
    try:
        summary = json.loads(summary_json_str)
        val_core_metrics = {}
        
        for key, value in summary.items():
            if key.startswith('val-core/') and '/acc/' in key and 'mean' in key:
                # Extract benchmark name and metric type
                parts = key.split('/')
                if len(parts) >= 3:
                    benchmark = parts[1]
                    metric_type = '/'.join(parts[2:])  # e.g., "acc/mean@1" or "acc/best@8/mean"
                    val_core_metrics[f"{benchmark}_{metric_type}"] = value
                    
        return val_core_metrics
    except:
        return {}

# Sample the first run's summary to understand the structure
sample_summary = """{\"_runtime\":241172.39391237,\"_step\":868,\"val-core/codegen__humaneval/acc/mean@1\":0.8963414634146342,\"val-core/codegen__livecodebench/acc/mean@1\":0.2831541218637993,\"val-core/codegen__mbpp/acc/mean@1\":0.825,\"val-core/logic__graph_logical_dataset/acc/mean@1\":0.987012987012987,\"val-core/logic__ordering_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1\":0.84,\"val-core/logic__zebra_puzzle_dataset/acc/mean@1\":0.41005998492248497,\"val-core/math__aime_repeated_8x/acc/best@8/mean\":0.5252333333333333,\"val-core/math__amc_repeated_4x/acc/best@4/mean\":0.7201927710843373,\"val-core/math__math/acc/mean@1\":0.86,\"val-core/simulation__arcagi1/acc/mean@1\":0.12,\"val-core/simulation__codeio/acc/mean@1\":0.15,\"val-core/stem__gpqa/acc/mean@1\":0.10606060606060606,\"val-core/stem__supergpqa/acc/mean@1\":0.43,\"val-core/table__hitab/acc/mean@1\":0.84,\"val-core/table__multihier/acc/mean@1\":0.595}"""

# Test the extraction function
test_metrics = extract_val_core_metrics(sample_summary)
print("Sample extracted metrics:")
for key, value in test_metrics.items():
    print(f"  {key}: {value}")

print(f"\nTotal metrics extracted: {len(test_metrics)}") code
```

```python
            "table__multihier_acc/mean@1": 0.605
        }

# Notion database column mapping
notion_columns = {
    "HumanEval": "codegen__humaneval_acc/mean@1",
    "LiveCodeBench": "codegen__livecodebench_acc/mean@1", 
    "MBPP": "codegen__mbpp_acc/mean@1",
    "Graph Logical": "logic__graph_logical_dataset_acc/mean@1",
    "Ordering Puzzle": "logic__ordering_puzzle_dataset_acc/mean@1",
    "Zebra Puzzle": "logic__zebra_puzzle_dataset_acc/mean@1",
    "AIME (8x)": "math__aime_repeated_8x_acc/best@8/mean",
    "AMC (4x)": "math__amc_repeated_4x_acc/best@4/mean",
    "MATH": "math__math_acc/mean@1",
    "ArcAgI1": "simulation__arcagi1_acc/mean@1",
    "CodeIO": "simulation__codeio_acc/mean@1",
    "GPQA": "stem__gpqa_acc/mean@1",
    "SuperGPQA": "stem__supergpqa_acc/mean@1",
    "HiTab": "table__hitab_acc/mean@1",
    "MultiHiertt": "table__multihier_acc/mean@1"
}

# Find the best scores for each benchmark across all runs
best_scores = {}
best_run_info = {}

for notion_col, metric_key in notion_columns.items():
    best_score = -1
    best_run = None
    best_step = None
    
    for run in runs_data:
        if metric_key in run["val_core_scores"]:
            score = run["val_core_scores"][metric_key]
            if score > best_score:
                best_score = score
                best_run = run["displayName"]
                best_step = run["step"]
    
    if best_run:
        best_scores[notion_col] = best_score
        best_run_info[notion_col] = {
            "score": best_score,
            "run": best_run,
            "step": best_step
        }

print("Best scores for each benchmark:")
print("="*50)
for notion_col in notion_columns.keys():
    if notion_col in best_scores:
        info = best_run_info[notion_col]
        print(f"{notion_col:15} | {info['score']:.4f} | {info['run']} | Step {info['step']}")
    else:
        print(f"{notion_col:15} | No data available")

print("\n" + "="*50)
print("Summary for Notion table update:")

# Calculate average scores for the best step format
for notion_col in notion_columns.keys():
    if notion_col in best_scores:
        info = best_run_info[notion_col]
        # For the "Best Step" column, we need to calculate average across available metrics at that step
        # Since we're looking at individual benchmark scores, the average would just be the score itself
        # But let's format it as requested: step(average acc)
        avg_score = info['score']  # This is the individual benchmark score
        best_step_format = f"{info['step']}({avg_score:.4f})"
        print(f"{notion_col}: {info['score']:.4f} (Best Step: {best_step_format})") code
```

```python
# Notion database column mapping
notion_columns = {
    "HumanEval": "codegen__humaneval_acc/mean@1",
    "LiveCodeBench": "codegen__livecodebench_acc/mean@1", 
    "MBPP": "codegen__mbpp_acc/mean@1",
    "Graph Logical": "logic__graph_logical_dataset_acc/mean@1",
    "Ordering Puzzle": "logic__ordering_puzzle_dataset_acc/mean@1",
    "Zebra Puzzle": "logic__zebra_puzzle_dataset_acc/mean@1",
    "AIME (8x)": "math__aime_repeated_8x_acc/best@8/mean",
    "AMC (4x)": "math__amc_repeated_4x_acc/best@4/mean",
    "MATH": "math__math_acc/mean@1",
    "ArcAgI1": "simulation__arcagi1_acc/mean@1",
    "CodeIO": "simulation__codeio_acc/mean@1",
    "GPQA": "stem__gpqa_acc/mean@1",
    "SuperGPQA": "stem__supergpqa_acc/mean@1",
    "HiTab": "table__hitab_acc/mean@1",
    "MultiHiertt": "table__multihier_acc/mean@1"
}

# Find the best scores for each benchmark across all runs
best_scores = {}
best_run_info = {}

for notion_col, metric_key in notion_columns.items():
    best_score = -1
    best_run = None
    best_step = None
    best_run_name = None
    
    for run in runs_data:
        if metric_key in run["val_core_scores"]:
            score = run["val_core_scores"][metric_key]
            if score > best_score:
                best_score = score
                best_run = run["displayName"]
                best_step = run["step"]
                best_run_name = run["name"]
    
    if best_run:
        best_scores[notion_col] = best_score
        best_run_info[notion_col] = {
            "score": best_score,
            "run": best_run,
            "run_name": best_run_name,
            "step": best_step
        }

print("Best scores for each benchmark:")
print("="*80)
print(f"{'Benchmark':<15} | {'Score':<8} | {'Run Name':<10} | {'Step':<6} | {'Display Name'}")
print("-"*80)
for notion_col in notion_columns.keys():
    if notion_col in best_scores:
        info = best_run_info[notion_col]
        print(f"{notion_col:<15} | {info['score']:<8.4f} | {info['run_name']:<10} | {info['step']:<6} | {info['run']}")
    else:
        print(f"{notion_col:<15} | No data available")

print("\n" + "="*80)
print("Data for Notion table update:")
print("="*80)

# Create the summary for updating the Notion table
notion_data = {}
for notion_col in notion_columns.keys():
    if notion_col in best_scores:
        info = best_run_info[notion_col]
        # For the "Best Step" column, format as step(average acc)
        avg_score = info['score']  # This is the individual benchmark score
        best_step_format = f"{info['step']}({avg_score:.4f})"
        
        notion_data[notion_col] = {
            "score": round(info['score'], 4),
            "best_step": best_step_format,
            "run_name": info['run_name']
        }
        
        print(f"{notion_col}:")
        print(f"  Score: {info['score']:.4f}")
        print(f"  Best Step: {best_step_format}")
        print(f"  Run: {info['run_name']} ({info['run']})")
        print()

print("Summary for Notion table (Column -> Value):")
print("="*50)
for col, data in notion_data.items():
    print(f"{col}: {data['score']} (Best Step: {data['best_step']})") code
```
